duke millen burgon braband coūties hasbrough flanders tiroll grace ioye felicitie wished god father lorde iesus christe almightie god merueilous creatour worlde beūteous conseruer moste noble prince hath graft naturall loue amitie nature creature one kinde chiefe succour one willyng moste orderly appere mannes nature societie hath beside benefite reason verie first beginnyng lawe prouided euen auncient enemie wilie▪ serpent deuill hath alwaie laied engine snare disorder confounde saied creation institution god many horrible kindes deuises either destroy vtterly el depraue thing impossible destroie suche sinister cauillations lose estimation least grace almightie god willed endued adourned chief roote whence spryngeth greatest part mannes felicitie infelicitie mortall life wedlocke spryng haue family realmes begūne enlarged finally florished preserued haue self family realmes aduaūced heigth felicitie perfection brought downe againe vtter ruine deuastation corrupting peruerting eternall lawe god decree nature earnestlie suche endewed spercle reuerence goddes honour pietie countrey charitie neighbour praie wishe moste instauntly state societie might bee honourablie begonne continued ended al degrées benefites therof might redounde throughout horriblenes abuse might bee vtterly euery banished circumspectly suche haue giftes god vtteraunce excityng mannes decaied corrupte nature woorde writyng preseruation thereof take hede imprudent vtteraunce thei defame thyng almightie god would haue estimation woorde hath pronounced honourable persones moste gracious godly soueraignes hath chaunced otherwise noble realme dominion late witte learnyng whereof nothing ought haue looked good witte learnyng haue vttered euill ignoraunce deprauatiō suche society part grace clergie iuste lawes realme enacted stablished confirmed good quiete state reposed straunge tyme reason noueltie diuerse yet perceiued many wisemen addition discipline insolencie yonger wiser might againste churche decree discipline worthie dissolued againe yet notwithstandyng importunitie read expresse wordes highnesse commission comprised article addressed grace spirituall administers bishop procured thus honour clergie preserued driue many twelue sixtene thousāde writer maketh accompte greate perill aduenture gettyng liuynges god knoweth meanes greate parte theim doen executed vttermoste beyonde farre iustice vpon greate nomber euen charge cure serued tenthes subsidie paied poincte receiuyng whiche labored deserued snatched mouthes preuentiōs furthermore though yet little certain thei knoweth god set vp intemperate tongue importunate ciuilian forgetting owne shame vilely blotte shame euer disablyng minister credence thereto endaunger theim body gooddes iustifiable prateth sed qui operit odium fraudulenter reuelabitur malicia eius consilio pro xxvj qui fodit foueam incidit eam qui voluit lapidem reuertetur ad ipsum couereth hatefull minde fraudulentlie doe hurte malice shalbe shewed whole congregation diggeth pitte shall fall therein hymself whirleth stone shall stumble vpon hym self witte wittie euer would seme learnyng hauyng vttred vniuersall yet euer would haue appere sone aunswered easte coste marie aucthoritie feared cause yet greate learning maie temper feare aucthorities perswadyng selues ye knowe aucthorities geuen ad edificationem non ad destructionem edifie destroie doubtyng nothyng wisedomes ye meane doe ye ye maie ye consider state cause standeth england difference tymes churche thei oportunities folowing grace whiche muche ensued yet libertie leape backe againe experience shewed inuicible difficilitie daielie intrications necessity liuyng companie plentie learned minister scarsitie yet makyng hereby sinistrall insinuation affirmyng plainly better hauyng thynges accompaniyng without whiche commendable de virgininitate yet plainly affirmyng againe saincte augustine ꝙ melior est scriptura dei veritas dei quam cuiusquam mēte carne virginitas hominis truthe god contra iouiniam contained scripture god better virginitie man whether minde fleshe man hierome concludyng ꝙ non sunt tanti virgines quanti necessarij sunt signifie vowe ergo englishe priestes bee votary haue proued matter bee farre vnlike crounes bee signes vowe rather thynges ye bee fondly deceiued trust ye doe perceiue tyme argue thus priestes crounes signifie suche vowe ergo signe englishe priestes votary thus nazareās shaued heere whē vowe doen paste priestes bee like nazareans ye saie ergo shauyng crounes thei bee paste vowe vnder vowe fourthe argument taciturnitie holdeth thus priestes ordered romane pontificall kepyng silence bushoppes proposicion binde selues taciturnitie vowe continencie ergo englishe priestes ordered owne potificall wherein suche proposition spoken bee v • taries furthermore owne difinition vowe bée deliberate aduised promise made god better entente purpose ye saie reason priestes profession vowe annexed votarie marrie thus argue englishe priestes make suche promise profession busshoppe requireth suche promise proposition doe include suche profession promise ergo maner orderyng englishe priestes votary
